Artur Masalcev. Software Engineering 1 year 4 group 1 subgroup 
Main task 2. Variant 8
This program solves 9x9 sudoku board using backtracking technique

PART 1 - INPUT

  Y, ROW
  ^
9 |  5 3 . . 7 . . . .
8 |  6 . . 1 9 5 . . .
7 |  . 9 8 . . . . 6 .
6 |  8 . . . 6 . . . 3
5 |  4 . . 8 . 3 . . 1
4 |  7 . . . 2 . . . 6
3 |  . 6 . . . . 2 8 .
2 |  . . . 4 1 9 . . 5
1 |  . . . . 8 . . 7 9
   ---------------------> X, COLUMN
     1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8 9
